    var ALTERNATE_CSS_BASE='http://cdn0.wn.com/or/ula/wn/2011-02-17/';
        function setCookie(cookieName, value) {
        var expiryDate = new Date();
        expiryDate.setTime(expiryDate.getTime()+(days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));

        jQuery.cookies.set(cookieName, value, {
            expiresAt: expiryDate
        });
    }

        var days = 365;
        var wnstyle_cookie = 'wnstyle';
        var bgcolor=false;
        var linkcolor=false;

        var switchStyle = function(styleName) {
            if(!jQuery(".themeswitch#"+styleName).length){
                styleName = 'white';
            }
            //jQuery('#videoquery0').val(jQuery('#videoquery0').val()+styleName+' ');
            var activeStylesheetIndex = -1;
            var activeStylesheet = null;
            var newActiveStylesheet = null;
            jQuery('link[@rel*=style][title]').each(
                function(i)
                {
                  if(this.getAttribute('rel').match('style')){
                    if (this.getAttribute('title') == styleName) {
                        this.disabled = false;
                        activeStylesheetIndex = i;
                        newActiveStylesheet = this;
                    }else{
                        if(!this.disabled && !activeStylesheet){
                            activeStylesheet = this;
                        }else{
                            this.disabled = true;
                        }
                    }
                  }
                }
            );
            if(activeStylesheetIndex == -1){
                //jQuery('link[@rel*=style][title=white]')[0].disabled=false;
                newActiveStylesheet = document.createElement("link");
                newActiveStylesheet.rel = 'stylesheet alternate';
                newActiveStylesheet.type = "text/css";
                newActiveStylesheet.title = styleName;
                newActiveStylesheet.href = ALTERNATE_CSS_BASE+styleName+'.css';
                newActiveStylesheet = document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(newActiveStylesheet);
                newActiveStylesheet.disabled=true;
                if(activeStylesheet){
                    activeStylesheet.disabled=true;
                }
                newActiveStylesheet.disabled=false;
                setTimeout(function () { // repeat if style didn't load
                    newActiveStylesheet.disabled=true;
                    if(activeStylesheet){
                        activeStylesheet.disabled=true;
                    }
                    newActiveStylesheet.disabled=false;
                }, 500);
            }else if(activeStylesheet && activeStylesheet.getAttribute('title') != styleName){
                newActiveStylesheet.disabled = true;
                activeStylesheet.disabled=true;
                newActiveStylesheet.disabled = false;
                // setTimeout(function () {
                //     newActiveStylesheet.disabled = false;
                // }, 100);
            }
            var bgstyle = 'transparent';
            var styleImage = jQuery.cookies.get('wnskin');
            if(styleImage){
                bgstyle = 'url(http://login.wn.com/media/skins/'+styleImage+')';
            }
            jQuery(".custom_bgr").css({'background' : bgstyle});
            setCookie(wnstyle_cookie, styleName, {'domain': '*.wn.com'});
        };

    jQuery(function() {
            var style = jQuery.cookies.get(wnstyle_cookie);
            if (style) {
                switchStyle(style);
            }

            // updating default colors from cookies
            if (jQuery.cookies.get('linkcolor')) { linkcolor = jQuery.cookies.get('linkcolor');}
            else { linkcolor = 'ffffff'; }
            if (jQuery.cookies.get('bgcolor')) { bgcolor = jQuery.cookies.get('bgcolor');}
            else { bgcolor = '000000'; }
            jQuery('#color-link div').css('backgroundColor', '#' + linkcolor);
            jQuery('#color-bg div').css('backgroundColor', '#' + bgcolor);

            jQuery('.themeswitch').click(function(event) {
                event.preventDefault();
                var style = jQuery(this).attr('id');
                switchStyle(style);
            });

    });

			    function async_load(){
			        var s = document.createElement("script");
			        s.type = "text/javascript";
			        s.async = true;
			        if (window.location.protocol == "https:")
			            s.src = "https://assets.pinterest.com/js/pinit.js";
			        else

			        x.parentNode.insertBefore(s, x);
			    }

			        window.attachEvent("onload", async_load);
			    else
			        window.addEventListener("load", async_load, false);

function getCookie(name) {
    var nameEQ = name + "=";
    var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
    for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {
        var c = ca[i];
        while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);
        if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
    }
    return null;
}

Network, has created this privacy statement in order to demonstrate our firm commitment to user privacy. The following discloses our information gathering and dissemination practices for wn.com, as well as e-mail newsletters.</p> <h3>1. Personal Information Collection and Use</h3> <p>We do not collect personally identifiable information about you, except when you provide it to us. For example, if you submit an inquiry to us or sign up for our newsletter, you may be asked to provide certain information such as your contact details (name, e-mail address, mailing address, etc.).</p> <p>When you submit your personally identifiable information through wn.com, you are giving your consent to the collection, use and disclosure of your personal information as set forth in this Privacy Policy. If you would prefer that we not collect any personally identifiable information from you, please do not provide us with any such information. We will not sell or rent your personally identifiable information to third parties without your consent, except as otherwise disclosed in this Privacy Policy. </p> <p>Except as otherwise disclosed in this Privacy Policy, we will use the information you provide us only for the purpose of responding to your inquiry or in connection with the service for which you provided such information. We may forward your contact information and inquiry to our affiliates and other divisions of our company that we feel can best address your inquiry or provide you with the requested service. We may also use the information you provide in aggregate form for internal business purposes, such as generating statistics and developing marketing plans. We may share or transfer such non-personally identifiable information with or to our affiliates, licensees, agents and partners.</p> <p>We may retain other companies and individuals to perform functions on our behalf. Such third parties may be provided with access to personally identifiable information needed to perform their functions, but may not use such information for any other purpose.</p> <p>In addition, we may disclose any information, including personally identifiable information, we deem necessary, in our sole discretion, to comply with any applicable law, regulation, legal proceeding or governmental request.</p> <h3>2.                             $(this).parent().find('.details-manual-order-confirm').hide();
                            new_vlist_value = parseInt($(this).val());
                            if (isNaN(new_vlist_value)) { return false; }
                            if (new_vlist_value == undefined) { return false; }
                            if (new_vlist_value == parseInt(init_vlist_value)) { return false; }
                            if (new_vlist_value < 0) { return false; }
                            if (new_vlist_value > pl_len) { return false; }
                            if (new_vlist_value == 0) { new_vlist_value = 1; }
                            $(this).parent().find('.details-manual-order-confirm').show();
                        });
                        // add the keypress event
                        $('#video-details .details-manual-order').live('keypress', function(e) {
                            if(e.keyCode == 13) {
                                var tmp = $('#video-details .video-desc').eq(init_vlist_value-1);
                                var target = $('#video-details .video-desc').eq(new_vlist_value-1);
                                var tmpc = tmp.clone(true);

                                target.find('.details-manual-order').val(init_vlist_value);
                                tmp.replaceWith(target);
                                var place = $('#video-details .video-desc').eq(new_vlist_value-1);
                                tmpc.insertBefore(place);

                                var items = $('#video-details .video-desc .details-manual-order');
                                for (var i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
                                    $(items[i]).val(i+1);
                                }

                                videoplayer.switchPlaylistItems(init_vlist_value, new_vlist_value);
                                init_vlist_value = false;
                                new_vlist_value = false;
                                $('#video-details .details-manual-order-confirm').hide();
                            }
                        });

        function initMVS(){
            var theForm = jQuery('#multi-video-search');
            theForm.submit(function(event) {
                event.preventDefault();
                var query = jQuery("#videoquery0").val();
                theForm.find('input[type=submit]').attr('disabled', 'disabled');
                jQuery.ajax({
                    data: {
                        t: 'worldnews/mvs.txt',
                        orderby: 'published',
                        corpus: 'current',
                        language_id: '1',
                        query: query
                    },
                    dataType: 'jsonp',
                    url: 'http://upge.wn.com/',
                    success: function(text) {
                            jQuery('#multiple_video').prepend(jQuery(text));
                    },
                    complete: function() {
                        theForm.find('input[type=submit]').attr('disabled', '');
                    }
                });
            });
        }
        jQuery(function() {
            initMVS();
        });

        function ie_find_flash(){
            for(var i=8; i>0; i--){
                flashVersion = 0;
                try{
                    var flash = new ActiveXObject("ShockwaveFlash.ShockwaveFlash." + i);
                    flashVersion = i;
                    return i;
                }
                catch(e){
                }
            }
            return 0;
        }
        function is_istuff() {
            var agent=navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
            var is_iPhone = (agent.indexOf('iphone')!=-1);
            var is_iPad = (agent.indexOf('ipad')!=-1);
            return (is_iPhone || is_iPad);
        }
        istuff = is_istuff();
        // hide the upper-block if Flash is not supported, for iPhone etc.
        var divname = 'upper-block';
        var element;
        var flash_supported = 0;
        if( document.getElementById ) // this is the way the standards work
            element = document.getElementById( divname );
        else if( document.all ) // this is the way old msie versions work
            element = document.all[divname];
        else if( document.layers ) // this is the way nn4 works
            element = document.layers[divname];

        // works on netscape and all sensible browsers
        if( navigator.mimeTypes["application/x-shockwave-flash"] ){
            flash_supported = 1;
        }else{
            flash_supported = ie_find_flash()
        }
        // iphone or ipad youtube videos can be embedded too

        if(!flash_supported && !istuff){
            element.style.display = 'none';
        }
        //-->

        jQuery(function(){
            window.tab2trigger = function(tab){
                var active_menu = $('ul#main-menu li a[id='+tab+']').parents('li');
                if(!active_menu.length){ // changed submenu
                    active_menu = $('.tabtrigger li.current-menu');
                }
                var submenu_link = active_menu.attr('id');
                $('.tabtrigger').children('li').removeClass('current-menu')
                $('.submenu').css('z-index', '10');
                var submenu = submenu_link && $(submenu_link);
                if(submenu && submenu.length && submenu.find('li').length > 1){
                    active_menu.addClass('current-menu')
                    submenu.css('z-index', '100');
                    submenu.slideDown('fast');
                    $('.submenu:not('+submenu_link+')').slideUp('fast');
                    $('.submenu-container').slideDown('fast');
                }else{
                    $('.submenu').slideUp('fast');
                    $('.submenu-container').slideUp('fast');
                }
            };
            window.activateTab = function(tab){
                jQuery('.tabtrigger').offscreentabs('activateTab', tab);
                tab2trigger('#'+tab); // activate
            };
            $('.tabtrigger li a').click(function() {
                var tab = $(this).attr('id');
                if(tab.substring(0,1) == '#'){
                    tab2trigger(tab);
                }
            });
            var replaces = {
                'image': 'slideshow',
                'people': 'related_people',
                'person': 'related_people',
                'place': 'related_places',
                'link': 'related_links',
                'site': 'related_links',
                'location': 'wiki0',
                'bio': 'wiki0',
                'book': 'books',
                'biography': 'wiki0',
                'biographie': 'wiki0',
                'wikipedia': 'wiki0',
                'wikipedia1': 'wiki0',
                'imdb': 'movieinfo',
                'movie': 'movieinfo',
                'new': 'expand',
                'shop': 'amazon_page',
                'shopping': 'amazon_page',
                'article': 'expand',
                'video': 'playlist1',
                'playlist': 'playlist1',
                'vid': 'playlist1',
                'detail': 'details1',
                'videodetail': 'details1',
                'video_detail': 'details1',
                'video-detail': 'details1',
                'travel': 'travel_booking',
                'booking': 'travel_booking',
                'travel_booking': 'travel_booking',
        };
        jQuery('.tabtrigger').offscreentabs();
        var part = document.location.hash.replace(/[#\/]*/,'').replace(/s$/,'');
        if(part in replaces){
            part = replaces[part];
            activateTab(part);
            var sup = $('ul#main-menu li a[id=#'+part+']');
            if(sup.attr('onclick')){ sup.attr('onclick')(); }
        }else{
            activateTab('highlights');
        }
    });
